<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-info, var(--color-fd-muted))" emoji="âš ï¸"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>In most cases, you shouldn&#x27;t directly <em>write</em> to the cache, which might cause undefined behaviors of SWR. If you need to manually mutate a key, please consider using the SWR APIs.<br/>
See also: <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/mutation">Mutation</a>, <a href="#reset-cache-between-test-cases" class="font-normal text-primary no-underline">Reset Cache Between Test Cases</a>.</p></div></div></div>
<p>By default, SWR uses a global cache to store and share data across all components. But you can also customize this behavior with the <code>provider</code> option of <code>SWRConfig</code>.</p>
<p>Cache providers are intended to enable SWR with more customized storages.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="cache-provider"><a data-card="" href="#cache-provider" class="peer">Cache Provider</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>A cache provider is Map-like object which matches the following TypeScript definition (which can be imported from <code>swr</code>):</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">interface</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Cache</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  get</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> |</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> undefined</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  set</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> void</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  delete</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> void</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  keys</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> IterableIterator</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<p>For example, a <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Map" class="font-normal text-primary no-underline">JavaScript Map</a> instance can be directly used as the cache provider for SWR.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="create-cache-provider"><a data-card="" href="#create-cache-provider" class="peer">Create Cache Provider</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The <code>provider</code> option of <code>SWRConfig</code> receives a function that returns a <a href="#cache-provider" class="font-normal text-primary no-underline">cache provider</a>. The provider will then be used by all SWR hooks inside that <code>SWRConfig</code> boundary. For example:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> useSWR, { SWRConfig } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;swr&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> App</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{{ </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">provider</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() }}&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Page</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">/&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<p>All SWR hooks inside <code>&lt;Page/&gt;</code> will read and write from that Map instance. You can also use other cache provider implementations as well for your specific use case.</p>
<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-info, var(--color-fd-muted))"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>In the example above, when the <code>&lt;App/&gt;</code> component is re-mounted, the provider will also be re-created. Cache providers should be put higher in the component tree, or outside of render.</p></div></div></div>

0 2.6-.7 3-1.9l-1.4-.2c-.2.7-.8 1-1.6 1-1.2 0-2-.8-2-2.1h5v-.5c0-2.6-1.5-3.6-3.1-3.6-2 0-3.3 1.5-3.3 3.7s1.3 3.6 3.4 3.6zm-2-4.3c0-1 .8-1.8 1.9-1.8 1 0 1.8.8 1.8 1.8H154zm6.5 4.2h1.4v-4.3c0-1 .7-1.6 1.7-1.6h.7v-1.3h-.6c-.8 0-1.5.5-1.8 1.2v-1h-1.4v7z"></path></svg></div>
<p>When nested, SWR hooks will use the upper-level cache provider. If there is no upper-level cache provider, it fallbacks to the default cache provider, which is an empty <code>Map</code>.</p>
<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-info, var(--color-fd-muted))" emoji="âš ï¸"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>If a cache provider is used, the global <code>mutate</code> will <strong>not</strong> work for SWR hooks under that <code>&lt;SWRConfig&gt;</code> boundary. Please use <a href="#access-current-cache-provider" class="font-normal text-primary no-underline">this</a> instead.</p></div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="access-current-cache-provider"><a data-card="" href="#access-current-cache-provider" class="peer">Access Current Cache Provider</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>When inside a React component, you need to use the <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/global-configuration#access-to-global-configurations"><code>useSWRConfig</code></a> hook to get access to the current cache provider as well as other configurations including <code>mutate</code>:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { useSWRConfig } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;swr&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Avatar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">cache</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">...</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">extraConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useSWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<p>If it&#x27;s not under any <code>&lt;SWRConfig&gt;</code>, it will return the default configurations.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="experimental-extend-cache-provider"><a data-card="" href="#experimental-extend-cache-provider" class="peer">Experimental: Extend Cache Provider</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-info, var(--color-fd-muted))" emoji="ðŸ§ª"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>This is an experimental feature, the behavior might change in future upgrades.</p></div></div></div>
<p>When multiple <code>&lt;SWRConfig&gt;</code> components are nested, cache provider can be extended.</p>
<p>The first argument for the <code>provider</code> function is the cache provider of the upper-level <code>&lt;SWRConfig&gt;</code> (or the default cache if there&#x27;s no parent <code>&lt;SWRConfig&gt;</code>), you can use it to extend the cache provider:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{{ </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">provider</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">cache</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> newCache }}&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="examples"><a data-card="" href="#examples" class="peer">Examples</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="localstorage-based-persistent-cache"><a data-card="" href="#localstorage-based-persistent-cache" class="peer">LocalStorage Based Persistent Cache</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>You might want to sync your cache to <code>localStorage</code>. Here&#x27;s an example implementation:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> localStorageProvider</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // When initializing, we restore the data from `localStorage` into a map.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">JSON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(localStorage.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">getItem</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;app-cache&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">||</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;[]&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">))</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // Before unloading the app, we write back all the data into `localStorage`.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  window.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">addEventListener</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;beforeunload&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> appCache</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> JSON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">stringify</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(Array.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(map.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">entries</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    localStorage.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">setItem</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;app-cache&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, appCache)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  })</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // We still use the map for write &amp; read for performance.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> map</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<p>Then use it as a provider:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{{ provider: localStorageProvider }}&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">App</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">/&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-info, var(--color-fd-muted))"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>As an improvement, you can also use the memory cache as a buffer, and write to <code>localStorage</code> periodically. You can also implement a similar layered cache with IndexedDB or WebSQL.</p></div></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="reset-cache-between-test-cases"><a data-card="" href="#reset-cache-between-test-cases" class="peer">Reset Cache Between Test Cases</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>When testing your application, you might want to reset the SWR cache between test cases. You can simply wrap your application with an empty cache provider. Here&#x27;s an example with Jest:</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">describe</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;test suite&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  it</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;test case&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    render</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{{ </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">provider</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() }}&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">App</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">/&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">})</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="modify-the-cache-data"><a data-card="" href="#modify-the-cache-data" class="peer">Modify the Cache Data</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<div class="flex gap-2 my-4 border p-3 ps-1 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground rounded-sm bg-transparent p-3! shadow-none [&amp;_div[role=&#x27;none&#x27;]]:hidden" style="--callout-color:var(--color-fd-error, var(--color-fd-muted))" emoji="ðŸš¨"><div role="none" class="w-0.5 bg-(--callout-color)/50 rounded-sm"></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide size-5 -me-0.5 fill-(--callout-color) text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="m15 9-6 6"></path><path d="m9 9 6 6"></path></svg><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin empty:hidden"><p>You should not write to the cache directly, it might cause undefined behavior.</p></div></div></div>
<p>You can use <a class="font-normal text-primary no-underline" href="/en/docs/mutation"><code>mutate</code></a> to modify the cache. For example, you can clear all cache data like the following.</p>
<div class="relative mb-6"><pre class="not-prose flex-1 overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border bg-background py-3 text-sm outline-none [&amp;&gt;code]:grid shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useSWRConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">mutate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// which cache keys are updated</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// update cache data to `undefined`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  { revalidate: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">false</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// do not revalidate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre><button data-slot="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&amp;_svg]:pointer-events-none [&amp;_svg:not([class*=&#x27;size-&#x27;])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&amp;_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50 size-9 absolute top-[5px] right-[5px] bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div>

github-dark\",\"style\":{\"--shiki-light\":\"#24292e\",\"--shiki-dark\":\"#e1e4e8\",\"--shiki-light-bg\":\"#fff\",\"--shiki-dark-bg\":\"#24292e\"},\"tabIndex\":\"0\",\"icon\":\"$95\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"span\",null,{\"className\":\"line\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"span\",null,{\"style\":{\"--shiki-light\":\"#D73A49\",\"--shiki-dark\":\"#F97583\"},\"children\":\"const\"}],[\"$\",\"span\",null,{\"style\":{\"--shiki-light\":\"#24292E\",\"--shiki-dark\":\"#E1E4E8\"},\"children\":\" \"}],\"$L96\",\"$L97\",\"$L98\",\"$L99\",\"$L9a\"]}],\"\\n\",\"$L9b\",\"\\n\",\"$L9c\",\"\\n\",\"$L9d\",\"\\n\",\"$L9e\",\"\\n\",\"$L9f\",\"\\n\",\"$La0\"]}]}]\n4a:[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"More information can be found \",[\"$\",\"$L10\",null,{\"className\":\"font-normal text-primary no-underline\",\"href\":\"/[lang]/docs/arguments#multiple-arguments\",\"children\":\"here\"}],\".\"]}]\n4b:[\"$\",\"$La1\",null,{\"items\":\"$undefined\"}]\na8:T14ee,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"# Cache\n\n\n\n\u003cCallout\u003e\n  Upgrade to the latest version (â‰¥ 1.0.0) to use this feature.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\n\u003cCallout emoji=\"âš ï¸\"\u003e\n  In most cases, you shouldn't directly *write* to the cache, which might cause undefined behaviors of SWR. If you need to manually mutate a key, please consider using the SWR APIs.\u003cbr /\u003e\n  See also: [Mutation](/docs/mutation), [Reset Cache Between Test Cases](#reset-cache-between-test-cases).\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\nBy default, SWR uses a global cache to store and share data across all components. But you can also customize this behavior with the `provider` option of `SWRConfig`.\n\nCache providers are intended to enable SWR with more customized storages.\n\n## Cache Provider\n\nA cache provider is Map-like object which matches the following TypeScript definition (which can be imported from `swr`):\n\n```typescript\ninterface Cache\u003cData\u003e {\n  get(key: string): Data | undefined\n  set(key: string, value: Data): void\n  delete(key: string): void\n  keys(): IterableIterator\u003cstring\u003e\n}\n```\n\nFor example, a [JavaScript Map](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Map) instance can be directly used as the cache provider for SWR.\n\n## Create Cache Provider\n\nThe `provider` option of `SWRConfig` receives a function that returns a [cache provider](#cache-provider). The provider will then be used by all SWR hooks inside that `SWRConfig` boundary. For example:\n\n```jsx\nimport useSWR, { SWRConfig } from 'swr'\n\nfunction App() {\n  return (\n    \u003cSWRConfig value={{ provider: () =\u003e new Map() }}\u003e\n      \u003cPage/\u003e\n    \u003c/SWRConfig\u003e\n  )\n}\n```\n\nAll SWR hooks inside `\u003cPage/\u003e` will read and write from that Map instance. You can also use other cache provider implementations as well for your specific use case.\n\n\u003cCallout\u003e\n  In the example above, when the `\u003cApp/\u003e` component is re-mounted, the provider will also be re-created. Cache providers should be put higher in the component tree, or outside of render.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv className=\"my-8\"\u003e\n  \u003cCache /\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\nWhen nested, SWR hooks will use the upper-level cache provider. If there is no upper-level cache provider, it fallbacks to the default cache provider, which is an empty `Map`.\n\n\u003cCallout emoji=\"âš ï¸\"\u003e\n  If a cache provider is used, the global `mutate` will **not** work for SWR hooks under that `\u003cSWRConfig\u003e` boundary. Please use [this](#access-current-cache-provider) instead.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\n## Access Current Cache Provider\n\nWhen inside a React component, you need to use the [`useSWRConfig`](/docs/global-configuration#access-to-global-configurations) hook to get access to the current cache provider as well as other configurations including `mutate`:\n\n```jsx\nimport { useSWRConfig } from 'swr'\n\nfunction Avatar() {\n  const { cache, mutate, ...extraConfig } = useSWRConfig()\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nIf it's not under any `\u003cSWRConfig\u003e`, it will return the default configurations.\n\n## Experimental: Extend Cache Provider\n\n\u003cCallout emoji=\"ðŸ§ª\"\u003e\n  This is an experimental feature, the behavior might change in future upgrades.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\nWhen multiple `\u003cSWRConfig\u003e` components are nested, cache provider can be extended.\n\nThe first argument for the `provider` function is the cache provider of the upper-level `\u003cSWRConfig\u003e` (or the default cache if there's no parent `\u003cSWRConfig\u003e`), you can use it to extend the cache provider:\n\n```jsx\n\u003cSWRConfig value={{ provider: (cache) =\u003e newCache }}\u003e\n  ...\n\u003c/SWRConfig\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### LocalStorage Based Persistent Cache\n\nYou might want to sync your cache to `localStorage`. Here's an example implementation:\n\n```jsx\nfunction localStorageProvider() {\n  // When initializing, we restore the data from `localStorage` into a map.\n  const map = new Map(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('app-cache') || '[]'))\n\n  // Before unloading the app, we write back all the data into `localStorage`.\n  window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () =\u003e {\n    const appCache = JSON.stringify(Array.from(map.entries()))\n    localStorage.setItem('app-cache', appCache)\n  })\n\n  // We still use the map for write \u0026 read for performance.\n  return map\n}\n```\n\nThen use it as a provider:\n\n```jsx\n\u003cSWRConfig value={{ provider: localStorageProvider }}\u003e\n  \u003cApp/\u003e\n\u003c/SWRConfig\u003e\n```\n\n\u003cCallout\u003e\n  As an improvement, you can also use the memory cache as a buffer, and write to `localStorage` periodically. You can also implement a similar layered cache with IndexedDB or WebSQL.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\n### Reset Cache Between Test Cases\n\nWhen testing your application, you might want to reset the SWR cache between test cases. You can simply wrap your application with an empty cache provider. Here's an example with Jest:\n\n```jsx\ndescribe('test suite', async () =\u003e {\n  it('test case', async () =\u003e {\n    render(\n      \u003cSWRConfig value={{ provider: () =\u003e new Map() }}\u003e\n        \u003cApp/\u003e\n      \u003c/SWRConfig\u003e\n    )\n  })\n})\n```\n\n### Modify the Cache Data\n\n\u003cCallout emoji=\"ðŸš¨\" type=\"error\"\u003e\n  You should not write to the cache directly, it might cause undefined behavior.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\nYou can use [`mutate`](/docs/mutation) to modify the cache. For example, you can clear all cache data like the following.\n\n```jsx\nconst { mutate } = useSWRConfig()\n\nmutate(\n  key =\u003e true, // which cache keys are updated\n  undefined, // update cache data to `undefined`\n  { revalidate: false } // do not revalidate\n)\n```\n\nMore information can be found [here](/docs/arguments#multiple-arguments).\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"4c:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"id\":\"nd-toc\",\"className\":\"sticky top-(--fd-docs-row-1)
